 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">11. <U>GOVERNING LAW</U> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">This Agreement shall be governed by the substantive laws (but not the choice of law rules) of the State of New York. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">12. <U>SUCCESSORS</U>
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Agreement shall be binding upon and inure to the benefit of the successors, assigns, and heirs of the respective parties. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">13. <U>DATA PRIVACY</U> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">By entering into this agreement, you
(i)&nbsp;authorize the Company, and any agent of the Company administering the Plan or providing Plan recordkeeping services, to disclose to the Company or any of its subsidiaries such information and data as the Company or any such subsidiary shall
request in order to facilitate the grant of RSUs and the administration of the Plan; (ii)&nbsp;waive any data privacy rights you may have with respect to such information; and (iii)&nbsp;authorize the Company to store and transmit such information
in electronic form. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">14. <U>ENTIRE AGREEMENT AND NO ORAL MODIFICATION OR WAIVER</U> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Agreement contains the entire understanding of the parties. This Agreement shall not be modified or amended except in writing duly signed by the parties, except that the Company may adopt a modification or
amendment to the Agreement that is not materially adverse to you in writing signed only by the Company. Any waiver of any right or failure to perform under this Agreement shall be in writing signed by the party granting the waiver and shall not be
deemed a waiver of any subsequent failure to perform. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">

</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2. Based on my knowledge, this quarterly report does not contain any untrue statement of a material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary to

flows of the registrant as of, and for, the periods presented in this quarterly report; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4. The registrant&#146;s other certifying officers and I are

the registrant and have: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a. designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and procedures to be designed under our
supervision, to ensure that material information relating to the registrant, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by others within those entities, particularly during the period in which this quarterly report is being

disclosure controls and procedures, as of the end of the period covered by this report based on such evaluation; and </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">d. disclosed in this report any
change in the registrant&#146;s internal control over financial reporting that occurred during the registrant&#146;s most recent fiscal quarter (the registrant&#146;s fourth fiscal quarter in the case of an annual report) that has materially
affected, or is reasonably likely to materially affect, the registrant&#146;s internal control over financial reporting; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5. The registrant&#146;s other
certifying officer and I have disclosed, based on our most recent evaluation, to the registrant&#146;s auditors and the audit committee of registrant&#146;s board of directors (or persons performing the equivalent function): </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a. all significant deficiencies and material weaknesses in the design or operation of internal controls, which are reasonably likely to adversely affect the
registrant&#146;s ability to record, process, summarize and report financial information; and </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">b. any fraud, whether or not material, that involves
management or other employees who have a significant role in the registrant&#146;s internal controls. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Date: May&nbsp;10, 2007 </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<DESCRIPTION>SECTION 906 CEO CERTIFICATION

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>EXHIBIT 32a. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Certification by the Chief Executive Officer Pursuant to 18 U. S. C. Section&nbsp;1350, as </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Adopted

with the requirements of Section&nbsp;13(a) or Section&nbsp;15(d) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and that the information contained in the Report fairly presents, in all material respects, the financial condition and results of
operations of Bristol-Myers Squibb Company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>EXHIBIT 32b. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Certification by the Chief Financial Officer Pursuant to 18 U. S. C. Section&nbsp;1350, as </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Adopted
Pursuant to Section&nbsp;906 of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Pursuant to 18 U.S.C. Section&nbsp;1350, I, Andrew R. J. Bonfield, hereby certify that,
to the best of my knowledge, Bristol-Myers Squibb Company&#146;s Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the quarter ended March&nbsp;31, 2007 (the &#147;Report&#148;), as filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on May&nbsp;10, 2007, fully
complies with the requirements of Section&nbsp;13(a) or Section&nbsp;15(d) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and that the information contained in the Report fairly presents, in all material respects, the financial condition and
results of operations of Bristol-Myers Squibb Company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
